<li id="menu-item-12776" class="menu-item menu-item-type-taxonomy menu-item-object-category menu-item-has-children menu-item-12776"><a href="https://www.spiciefoodie.com/category/holidays/"><span class="nav-drop-title-wrap">Holidays<span class="dropdown-nav-toggle"><span class="kadence-svg-iconset svg-baseline"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="kadence-svg-icon kadence-arrow-down-svg" fill="currentColor" version="1.1" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><title>Expand</title><path d="M5.293 9.707l6 6c0.391 0.391 1.024 0.391 1.414 0l6-6c0.391-0.391 0.391-1.024 0-1.414s-1.024-0.391-1.414 0l-5.293 5.293-5.293-5.293c-0.391-0.391-1.024-0.391-1.414 0s-0.391 1.024 0 1.414z"></path>
				</svg></span></span></span></a>

						<div class="content-wrap">
				<article id="post-3037" class="entry content-bg single-entry post-3037 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-announcements grow-content-main">
	<div class="entry-content-wrap">
		<header class="entry-header post-title title-align-inherit title-tablet-align-inherit title-mobile-align-inherit">
	<div class="kadence-breadcrumbs rankmath-bc-wrap"><nav aria-label="breadcrumbs" class="rank-math-breadcrumb"><p><a href="https://www.spiciefoodie.com">Home</a><span class="separator"> - </span><a href="https://www.spiciefoodie.com/recipe-index/">Recipe Index</a><span class="separator"> - </span><a href="https://www.spiciefoodie.com/category/announcements/">Announcements</a></p></nav></div><h1 class="entry-title">Spicie Foodie, The Mobile App</h1><div class="entry-meta entry-meta-divider-customicon">
	<span class="posted-by"><span class="meta-label">By</span><span class="author vcard"><a class="url fn n" href="https://www.spiciefoodie.com/about/">Nancy Lopez-McHugh</a></span></span>					<span class="posted-on">
						<span class="kadence-svg-iconset"><svg class="kadence-svg-icon kadence-hours-alt-svg" fill="currentColor" version="1.1" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><title>Hours</title><path d="M23 12c0-3.037-1.232-5.789-3.222-7.778s-4.741-3.222-7.778-3.222-5.789 1.232-7.778 3.222-3.222 4.741-3.222 7.778 1.232 5.789 3.222 7.778 4.741 3.222 7.778 3.222 5.789-1.232 7.778-3.222 3.222-4.741 3.222-7.778zM21 12c0 2.486-1.006 4.734-2.636 6.364s-3.878 2.636-6.364 2.636-4.734-1.006-6.364-2.636-2.636-3.878-2.636-6.364 1.006-4.734 2.636-6.364 3.878-2.636 6.364-2.636 4.734 1.006 6.364 2.636 2.636 3.878 2.636 6.364zM11 6v6c0 0.389 0.222 0.727 0.553 0.894l4 2c0.494 0.247 1.095 0.047 1.342-0.447s0.047-1.095-0.447-1.342l-3.448-1.723v-5.382c0-0.552-0.448-1-1-1s-1 0.448-1 1z"></path>
				</svg></span><span class="meta-label">Posted on</span><time class="entry-date published" datetime="2012-02-08T07:02:42-06:00" itemprop="datePublished">February 8, 2012</time><time class="updated" datetime="2017-07-09T20:54:55-05:00" itemprop="dateModified">July 9, 2017</time>					</span>
										<span class="updated-on">
						<span class="kadence-svg-iconset"><svg class="kadence-svg-icon kadence-hours-alt-svg" fill="currentColor" version="1.1" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><title>Hours</title><path d="M23 12c0-3.037-1.232-5.789-3.222-7.778s-4.741-3.222-7.778-3.222-5.789 1.232-7.778 3.222-3.222 4.741-3.222 7.778 1.232 5.789 3.222 7.778 4.741 3.222 7.778 3.222 5.789-1.232 7.778-3.222 3.222-4.741 3.222-7.778zM21 12c0 2.486-1.006 4.734-2.636 6.364s-3.878 2.636-6.364 2.636-4.734-1.006-6.364-2.636-2.636-3.878-2.636-6.364 1.006-4.734 2.636-6.364 3.878-2.636 6.364-2.636 4.734 1.006 6.364 2.636 2.636 3.878 2.636 6.364zM11 6v6c0 0.389 0.222 0.727 0.553 0.894l4 2c0.494 0.247 1.095 0.047 1.342-0.447s0.047-1.095-0.447-1.342l-3.448-1.723v-5.382c0-0.552-0.448-1-1-1s-1 0.448-1 1z"></path>
				</svg></span><span class="meta-label">Updated on</span><time class="entry-date published updated" datetime="2017-07-09T20:54:55-05:00" itemprop="dateModified">July 9, 2017</time>					</span>
					</div><!-- .entry-meta -->
</header><!-- .entry-header -->

<div class="entry-content single-content">
	<p><img fetchpriority="high" width="284" height="510" decoding="async" class="aligncenter" title="" src="https://www.spiciefoodie.com/blogimages/MobApp/SF_MobileApp.jpg" alt="Spicie Foodie, Mobile App, Food, Recipes" /><br />
I have some really exciting news to share, Spicie Foodie has gone mobile. What exactly does that mean? It means that for those of you visiting Spicie Foodie on your Smartphones, iPad, and or Android Tablets reading Spicie Foodie just become a little bit easier.</p>
<p>The Mobile App is completely free of charge, all you need to do is download it onto your mobile device.<br />
<img width="272" height="486" decoding="async" class="aligncenter" title="" src="https://www.spiciefoodie.com/blogimages/MobApp/spiciefoodie_mobapp.png" alt="Spicie Foodie, Mobile App, Food, Recipes" /></p>
<p>Simply type the following link into your device&#8217;s web browser, <a title="Spicie Foodie Mobile App" href="http://spiciefoodie.mobapp.at/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">http://spiciefoodie.mobapp.at/</a> OR you can also scan the QR Code. Once you&#8217;ve typed in the address or scanned the QRC you can click &#8220;Get it now&#8221; to download the app onto your device.<br />
<img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="http://storage.conduit.com/Mobile/34/9e/3496e2b8-759e-480e-99b7-324ce56474db/Images/50ffe31e-74db-4de9-ac18-adbcae4e6761.png" alt="" width="175" height="175" /></p>
<p>This is the App&#8217;s Icon that will appear on your device. Once installed simply click on it to start reading the latest Spicie Foodie article.<br />
<img width="350" height="350" decoding="async" class="aligncenter" title="" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20350%20350'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Spicie Foodie, Mobile App, Food, Recipes" data-lazy-src="https://www.spiciefoodie.com/blogimages/MobApp/AppIcon.jpg" /><noscript><img width="350" height="350" decoding="async" class="aligncenter" title="" src="https://www.spiciefoodie.com/blogimages/MobApp/AppIcon.jpg" alt="Spicie Foodie, Mobile App, Food, Recipes" /></noscript></p>
<p>The App was designed to be compatible with IOS (iPhone,iPad), Android, Blackberry and BADA. But I can&#8217;t give 100% guarantee that it will work perfectly on all those operating systems.<br />
<img width="284" height="510" decoding="async" class="alignleft" title="" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20284%20510'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Spicie Foodie, Mobile App, Food, Recipes" data-lazy-src="https://www.spiciefoodie.com/blogimages/MobApp/iPhone_scn.jpg" /><noscript><img width="284" height="510" decoding="async" class="alignleft" title="" src="https://www.spiciefoodie.com/blogimages/MobApp/iPhone_scn.jpg" alt="Spicie Foodie, Mobile App, Food, Recipes" /></noscript><img width="279" height="510" decoding="async" title="" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20279%20510'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Spicie Foodie, Mobile App, Food, Recipes" data-lazy-src="https://www.spiciefoodie.com/blogimages/MobApp/Android_scn.jpg" /><noscript><img width="279" height="510" decoding="async" title="" src="https://www.spiciefoodie.com/blogimages/MobApp/Android_scn.jpg" alt="Spicie Foodie, Mobile App, Food, Recipes" /></noscript></p>
<p>I own an Android tablet and this is a screenshot sample of the App. The design is basic and it includes Recipes, About Us, Questions, Twitter Feed, and a small Photos section. At this time the app doesn&#8217;t not have the avility to leave a comment on a recipe/post. But if you would like to leave a comment simply click the &#8220;View Original Post&#8221;, you will be redirected to the regular site.<br />
<img width="438" height="700" decoding="async" class="aligncenter" title="" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20438%20700'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Spicie Foodie, Mobile App, Food, Recipes" data-lazy-src="https://www.spiciefoodie.com/blogimages/MobApp/Android_tablet.png" /><noscript><img width="438" height="700" decoding="async" class="aligncenter" title="" src="https://www.spiciefoodie.com/blogimages/MobApp/Android_tablet.png" alt="Spicie Foodie, Mobile App, Food, Recipes" /></noscript></p>
<p style="text-align: center;">This is the iPad screenshot sample.<br />
<img width="600" height="461" decoding="async" class="aligncenter" title="" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20600%20461'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Spicie Foodie, Mobile App, Food, Recipes" data-lazy-src="https://www.spiciefoodie.com/blogimages/MobApp/iPad_samp.jpg" /><noscript><img width="600" height="461" decoding="async" class="aligncenter" title="" src="https://www.spiciefoodie.com/blogimages/MobApp/iPad_samp.jpg" alt="Spicie Foodie, Mobile App, Food, Recipes" /></noscript></p>
<p><span style="color: #c0c0c0;"><strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;">Consider this a BETA version with many more improvements and features to come!</span> If you experience any problems try to go easy on me as I am not yet a Mobile App expert :) (But I am a gadget geek. Evidence below) Thanks everyone!</strong></span></p>
<p><img width="505" height="600" decoding="async" class="aligncenter" title="" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20505%20600'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Spicie Foodie, Mobile App, Food, Recipes" data-lazy-src="https://www.spiciefoodie.com/blogimages/MobApp/devices.png" /><noscript><img width="505" height="600" decoding="async" class="aligncenter" title="" src="https://www.spiciefoodie.com/blogimages/MobApp/devices.png" alt="Spicie Foodie, Mobile App, Food, Recipes" /></noscript></p>
<p>Yes, honey I really do need all of these gadgets. Just kidding these aren&#8217;t all mine&#8230;okay maybe most, but not all&#8230;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p><span style="border-top-left-radius: 2px; border-top-right-radius: 2px; border-bottom-right-radius: 2px; border-bottom-left-radius: 2px; text-indent: 20px; width: auto; padding: 0px 4px 0px 0px; text-align: center; font-style: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: bold; font-size: 11px; line-height: 20px; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, sans-serif; color: #ffffff; background-image: url(data:image/svg+xml; <div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-columncbbedc-e3"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><style></style>
<h3 class="kt-adv-heading2f9317-82 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading2f9317-82">Hi, I'm Nancy Lopez!</h3>


<style></style>
<div class="wp-block-kadence-image kb-image05da76-88"><figure class="aligncenter size-large kb-image-is-ratio-size"><div class="kb-is-ratio-image kb-image-ratio-square"><img decoding="async" width="1013" height="1800" src="https://www.spiciefoodie.com/wp-content/wp_uploads/2025/09/spicie-foodie-nancy-bio-pic-1013x1800.jpg" alt="Nacy Lopez Author and creator of Spicie Foodie profile picture" class="kb-img wp-image-12487" srcset="https://www.spiciefoodie.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/spicie-foodie-nancy-bio-pic-1013x1800.jpg 1013w, https://www.spiciefoodie.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/spicie-foodie-nancy-bio-pic-591x1050.jpg 591w, https://www.spiciefoodie.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/spicie-foodie-nancy-bio-pic-768x1365.jpg 768w, https://www.spiciefoodie.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/spicie-foodie-nancy-bio-pic-864x1536.jpg 864w, https://www.spiciefoodie.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/spicie-foodie-nancy-bio-pic.jpg 1125w" sizes="(max-width: 1013px) 100vw, 1013px" /></div></figure></div>



<p class="has-text-align-center">Welcome to Spicie Foodie, where you’ll find recipes from around the World! I love to share spicy dishes from Mexico, India, Thailand, as well as less spicy dishes from all over the world. All of my recipes are healthy, fresh, delicious, and guaranteed to spice up your kitchen!<br><a href="https://www.spiciefoodie.com/about/" data-type="page" data-id="5">Read more about me here</a>.</p>
